	desc = CZE_czech.1.d
	picture = GFX_court

		name = CZE_czech.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.1.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_czech.3
	title = CZE_czech.3.t
	desc = CZE_czech.3.d
	picture = GFX_internal_faction_business_purchase

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.3.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.3.o1 executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = CZE_skoda_increased_production_tooltip

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_i
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_ii
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb2_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iii
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb3_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iv
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb4_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.3.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.3.o2 executed"
		add_ideas = CZE_skoda_productivity_improved_idea

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_czech.19
	title = CZE_czech.19.t
	desc = CZE_czech.19.d
	picture = GFX_pol_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.19.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.19.o1 executed"
		CZE = {
			country_event = CZE_czech.20
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		army_experience = 30
		add_command_power = 20
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = CZE_czech_polish_military_cooperation
			cost_reduction = 0.2
			uses = 3
			category = CAT_land_doctrine
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				add = -35
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.19.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.19.o2 executed"
		CZE = {
			country_event = CZE_czech.21
		}
		add_war_support = -0.08
		add_stability = 0.06

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				add = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

### TV Crisis ###
country_event = {
	id = CZE_TV_Crisis.01
	title = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.t
	desc = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.d
	picture = GFX_czech_tv

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_TV_Crisis.01.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.02 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.03 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_TV_Crisis.01.b executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.04 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
				70 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.05 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

country_event = {
	id = czech_skoda.1
	title = czech_skoda.1.t
	desc = czech_skoda.1.d
	picture = GFX_german_emmigration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.1.o1 executed"

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_cars_stockpile > 999 }
		}

		set_variable = { car_generation = 1 }
		CZE_skoda_export_option_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.1.o2 executed"

		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_ii
			check_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb2_cars_stockpile > 999 }
		}

		set_variable = { car_generation = 2 }
		CZE_skoda_export_option_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.1.o3 executed"

		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iii
			check_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb3_cars_stockpile > 999 }
		}

		set_variable = { car_generation = 3 }
		CZE_skoda_export_option_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.1.o4
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.1.o4 executed"

		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iv
			check_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb4_cars_stockpile > 999 }
		}

		set_variable = { car_generation = 4 }
		CZE_skoda_export_option_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.1.o5
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.1.o5 executed"

		CZE_skoda_clear_export_data_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = czech_skoda.2
	title = czech_skoda.2.t
	desc = czech_skoda.2.d
	picture = GFX_politics_talks

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = czech_skoda.2.o1.german
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: czech_skoda.2.o1.german executed"

		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CZE_skoda_export_german_gen1_flag
		}

		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_timed_idea = { idea = CZE_skoda_superb_i_bought_idea days = 30 }
		clr_country_flag = CZE_skoda_export_german_gen1_flag

		CZE = {
			subtract_from_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_cars_stockpile = 1000 }
			set_country_flag = { flag = CZE_skoda_cars_sold_to_germany days = 30 value = 1 }
			clear_variable = CZE_skoda_superb_cars_sell_german_var
			country_event = czech_skoda.3
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { CZE.CZE_skoda_superb_german_demand > 90 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 1.35 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_cars_treasury = 1.35 }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 1.125 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_cars_treasury = 1.125 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CZE_volkswagen_group_skoda_idea
				}
				add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_german_demand = -2 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_german_demand = -4 }
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = var:CZE.CZE_skoda_superb_german_demand
			}
		}
	}

	title = CZE_petr_pavel_event.20.t
	desc = CZE_petr_pavel_event.20.d
	picture = GFX_Iraqi_Insurgency

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_petr_pavel_event.20.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_petr_pavel_event.20.a executed"
		add_to_variable = { petr_pavel_training_points = 12 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = petr_pavel_training_points
			max = 120
		}
		add_to_variable = { petr_pavel_card_three_points = 8 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = petr_pavel_card_three_points
			max = 100
		}
		add_to_variable = { petr_pavel_card_one_points = 8 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = petr_pavel_card_one_points
			max = 100
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = QAT
				modifier = CZE_petr_pavel_completed_mission_six
			}
		}
		army_experience = 15

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_airforce_event.1
	title = CZE_airforce_event.1.t
	desc = CZE_airforce_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_fighter_jet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_airforce_event.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_airforce_event.1.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_strike_airframe_1
				variant_name = "Su-22M5 Fitter"
				amount = -15
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = Strike_fighter1
				amount = -15
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 8 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_airforce_event.1.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_airforce_event.1.b executed"
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = small_plane_strike_airframe_2
				amount = 15
				variant_name = "Aero L-159"
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = L_Strike_fighter3
				amount = 15
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -12 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_airforce_event.2
	title = CZE_airforce_event.2.t
	desc = CZE_airforce_event.2.d
	picture = GFX_fighter_jet

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_airforce_event.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_airforce_event.2.a executed"
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				CZE_exists_not_at_war_not_embargoing = yes
			}

			USA = {
				CZE_exists_not_at_war_not_embargoing = yes
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = large_plane_air_transport_airframe_1
				variant_name = "C-130 Hercules"
				amount = 10
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = transport_plane1
				amount = 10
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = CZE_airforce_event.3
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 13.5 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -13.5 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = CZE_monarchy_event.21
	title = CZE_monarchy_event.21.t
	desc = CZE_monarchy_event.21.des
	picture = GFX_news_press_conference

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = CZE_monarchy_event.21.a
		trigger = { original_tag = CZE }

		custom_effect_tooltip = CZE_royal_coronation_ready_TT

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CZE_president_resign
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.21.a executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.21.b

		trigger = {
			original_tag = AUS
			CZE = { has_completed_focus = CZE_seek_support_from_austria }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.21.b executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.21.c

		trigger = {
			CZE = { has_completed_focus = CZE_seek_support_from_hungary }
			original_tag = HUN
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.21.c executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.21.d

		trigger = { original_tag = SLO }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.21.d executed"
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.21.e

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = CZE
				if = {
					CZE = { has_completed_focus = CZE_seek_support_from_austria }
					original_tag = AUS
				}
				if = {
					CZE = { has_completed_focus = CZE_seek_support_from_hungary }
					original_tag = HUN
				}
				original_tag = SLO
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.21.e executed"
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_monarchy_event.23
	title = CZE_monarchy_event.23.t
	desc = CZE_monarchy_event.23.d
	picture = GFX_habsburgs

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.23.a


		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NATO_member
			}
			NATO_leave = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CSTO_member
			}
			CSTO_leave = yes
		}
		else = {
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		CZE = { add_to_faction = ROOT }


		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > 50
					}
				}
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					has_government = FROM
				}
				add = 30
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.23.a executed"
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_monarchy_event.23.b

		CZE = { country_event = CZE_monarchy_event.25 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > 50
					}
				}
				add = -10
			}
			modifier = {
				ROOT = {
					has_government = FROM
				}
				add = -30
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_monarchy_event.23.b executed"
	}
}

# UK event see "Encourage British Royal Family support" focus
country_event = {
	id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3
	title = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.t
	desc = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.d

	picture = GFX_politics_talks

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.a

		BEL = { country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4 days = 1} }

		CZE = { country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.14} }

		ROOT = {
			country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.16 days = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -2 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { is_on_continent = europe }
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 }
					AND = {
						original_tag = DEN
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LUX
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = MNC
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = HOL
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = NOR
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = SWE
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = SPR
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
				NOT = { original_tag = CZE }
				NOT = { original_tag = BEL }
			}
			country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.5 }
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.a executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.b

		CZE = { country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.15 } }

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.3.b executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

}

#BEL event if the UK accepts
country_event = {
	id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4
	title = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.t
	desc = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.d

	picture = GFX_politics_negotiations

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = BEL
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.a

		trigger = {
			BEL = { NOT = { has_government = communism} }
		}

		BEL = { set_country_flag = CZE_BEL_plan }
		CZE = { set_country_flag = CZE_BEL_plan }

		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CZE_future_of_monarchies
			days = 180
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.a executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	# Secret option for Belgium if communist
	option = {
		name = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.b

		trigger = {
			BEL = {
				has_government = communism
			}
		}

		CZE = {
			complete_national_focus = CZE_visit_belgium
			complete_national_focus = CZE_initiate_the_return_of_the_archduke_lorenz_of_austria-este
			country_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.20 days = 15 }
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.4.b executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

}

# AUS event for the ascens to power of monarchist. see Kingdown of Austria focus
country_event = {
	id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.9
	title = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.9.t
	desc = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.9.d

	picture = GFX_habsburgs

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.9.a

		CZE = {
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = AUS
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}

		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = BEL
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}

		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = AUS
			relation = guarantee
			active = yes
		}
	}
		BEL = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = AUS
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}

			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CZE
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
		}

		AUS = {
			clear_array = ruling_party
			clear_array = gov_coalition_array

			add_to_array = { ruling_party = 23 }

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = nationalist
				elections_allowed = no
				}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CZE
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}

			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = BEL
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CZE_AUS_payment_to_habsburgs }
				remove_ideas = CZE_AUS_payment_to_habsburgs
			}
		}

		news_event = { id = CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.13 days = 1 }

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_AUS_monarchy_event.9.a executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

		name = CZE_HUN_monarchy_event.44.a

			idea = CZE_HUN_fallen_government
			days = 180
		}

		for_each_loop = {
			array = neighbors
			value = bordering_country
			var:bordering_country = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23} } }
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = CZE_increase_border_patrols
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_HUN_monarchy_event.44.a executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

				picture = "Viktor_Orban.dds"

				ideology = Monarchist
				traits = {
					CZE_a_puppet_king
				}
			}
		}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_HUN_monarchy_event.45.a executed"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}
